-- Patch Provenance ----------------------------------------------------------
|  P013 [AG_COVERAGE_H003] lever=6 (SQL Expressions) type=add_sql_snippet_expression root_cause=wrong_join_spec: The generated SQL uses RANK() which can return more than 10 rows when there are ties, resulting in 16 rows instead of 10. It should use ROW_NUMBER() or LIMIT 10 to strictly return the top 10 origin-destination pairs. Additionally, the IS NOT NULL filters on ORIG_AIRPORT_CD and DEST_AIRPORT_CD are defensive and acceptable, but the IS NOT NULL on FARE_BASIS_CD combined with LEFT JOIN could subtly change results. The core issue is using RANK() instead of a strict top-10 limit.

--- Q17: q17 ----------------------------------------------------------------
| Question:  "What are the top 10 origin-destination airport pairs by total number of coupons, along with the most common fare basis code for each route?"
|
| Genie SQL:
|   WITH route_counts AS (
  SELECT 
    ORIG_AIRPORT_CD, 
    DEST_AIRPORT_CD, 
    COUNT(*) AS coupon_count
  FROM prashanth_subrahmanyam_catalog.dev_prashanth_subrahmanyam_evcr_bronze.tkt_coupon
  WHERE ORIG_AIRPORT_CD IS NOT NULL AND DEST_AIRPORT_CD IS NOT NULL
  GROUP BY ORIG_AIRPORT_CD, DEST_AIRPORT_CD
),
most_common_fare AS (
  SELECT 
    ORIG_AIRPORT_CD, 
    DEST_AIRPORT_CD, 
    FARE_BASIS_CD, 
    COUNT(*) AS fare_count,
    ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY ORIG_AIRPORT_CD, DEST_AIRPORT_CD ORDER BY COUNT(*) DESC) AS rn
  FROM prashanth_subrahmanyam_catalog.dev_prashanth_subrahmanyam_evcr_bronze.tkt_coupon
  WHERE ORIG_AIRPORT_CD IS NOT NULL AND DEST_AIRPORT_CD IS NOT NULL AND FARE_BASIS_CD IS NOT NULL
  GROUP BY ORIG_AIRPORT_CD, DEST_AIRPORT_CD, FARE_BASIS_CD
)
SELECT 
  rc.ORIG_AIRPORT_CD, 
  rc.DEST_AIRPORT_CD, 
  rc.coupon_count, 
  mcf.FARE_BASIS_CD AS most_common_fare_basis_cd
FROM route_counts rc
LEFT JOIN most_common_fare mcf
  ON rc.ORIG_AIRPORT_CD = mcf.ORIG_AIRPORT_CD
  AND rc.DEST_AIRPORT_CD = mcf.DEST_AIRPORT_CD
  AND mcf.rn = 1
QUALIFY RANK() OVER (ORDER BY rc.coupon_count DESC) <= 10
ORDER BY rc.coupon_count DESC, rc.ORIG_AIRPORT_CD, rc.DEST_AIRPORT_CD
| Genie Status: MessageStatus.COMPLETED
| Genie Analysis: The top 10 origin-destination airport pairs by total number of coupons, along with their most common fare basis code, are as follows (using all available data):

- **ANC to ATL**: 27 coupons, most com
|
| Ground Truth SQL:
|   WITH route_counts AS (
  SELECT
    ORIG_AIRPORT_CD,
    DEST_AIRPORT_CD,
    COUNT(*) AS total_coupons
  FROM prashanth_subrahmanyam_catalog.dev_prashanth_subrahmanyam_evcr_bronze.tkt_coupon
  GROUP BY ORIG_AIRPORT_CD, DEST_AIRPORT_CD
  ORDER BY total_coupons DESC
  LIMIT 10
),
fare_basis_counts AS (
  SELECT
    ORIG_AIRPORT_CD,
    DEST_AIRPORT_CD,
    FARE_BASIS_CD,
    COUNT(*) AS fb_count,
    ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY ORIG_AIRPORT_CD, DEST_AIRPORT_CD ORDER BY COUNT(*) DESC) AS rn
  FROM prashanth_subrahmanyam_catalog.dev_prashanth_subrahmanyam_evcr_bronze.tkt_coupon
  GROUP BY ORIG_AIRPORT_CD, DEST_AIRPORT_CD, FARE_BASIS_CD
)
SELECT
  rc.ORIG_AIRPORT_CD,
  rc.DEST_AIRPORT_CD,
  rc.total_coupons,
  fbc.FARE_BASIS_CD AS most_common_fare_basis_cd
FROM route_counts rc
JOIN fare_basis_counts fbc
  ON rc.ORIG_AIRPORT_CD = fbc.ORIG_AIRPORT_CD
  AND rc.DEST_AIRPORT_CD = fbc.DEST_AIRPORT_CD
  AND fbc.rn = 1
ORDER BY rc.total_coupons DESC
|

  Q1: [q1] "What are the distinct tax codes and the total tax amount for each from the tax d" — LOGICAL PASS (both_correct)

--- Q2: q2 ------------------------------------------------------------------
| Question:  "How many coupon status transitions occurred per month, and what are the most frequent previous-to-new status change patterns in the coupon history?"
|
| Genie SQL:
|   WITH monthly_transitions AS (
  SELECT DATE_TRUNC('MONTH', TRANSACTION_DTTM) AS transition_month, COUNT(*) AS transition_count
  FROM prashanth_subrahmanyam_catalog.dev_prashanth_subrahmanyam_evcr_bronze.tkt_coupon_history
  WHERE TRANSACTION_DTTM IS NOT NULL
  GROUP BY DATE_TRUNC('MONTH', TRANSACTION_DTTM)
),
status_change_patterns AS (
  SELECT PREVIOUS_COUPON_STATUS_CD, NEW_COUPON_STATUS_CD, COUNT(*) AS pattern_count
  FROM prashanth_subrahmanyam_catalog.dev_prashanth_subrahmanyam_evcr_bronze.tkt_coupon_history
  WHERE PREVIOUS_COUPON_STATUS_CD IS NOT NULL AND NEW_COUPON_STATUS_CD IS NOT NULL
  GROUP BY PREVIOUS_COUPON_STATUS_CD, NEW_COUPON_STATUS_CD
  ORDER BY pattern_count DESC
  LIMIT 20
)
SELECT 'Monthly Transitions' AS category, transition_month AS period, NULL AS previous_status, NULL AS new_status, transition_count AS count FROM monthly_transitions
UNION ALL
SELECT 'Top Status Change Patterns' AS category, NULL AS period, PREVIOUS_COUPON_STATUS_CD AS previous_status, NEW_COUPON_STATUS_CD AS new_status, pattern_count AS count FROM status_change_patterns

| Question:  "What are the top 10 origin-destination airport pairs by total number of coupons, along with the most common fare basis code for each route?"
|
| Genie SQL:
|   WITH route_stats AS ( SELECT ORIG_AIRPORT_CD, DEST_AIRPORT_CD, COUNT(*) AS coupon_count FROM prashanth_subrahmanyam_catalog.dev_prashanth_subrahmanyam_evcr_bronze.tkt_coupon WHERE ORIG_AIRPORT_CD IS NOT NULL AND DEST_AIRPORT_CD IS NOT NULL GROUP BY ORIG_AIRPORT_CD, DEST_AIRPORT_CD ), fare_mode AS ( SELECT ORIG_AIRPORT_CD, DEST_AIRPORT_CD, FARE_BASIS_CD, COUNT(*) AS fare_count, ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY ORIG_AIRPORT_CD, DEST_AIRPORT_CD ORDER BY COUNT(*) DESC) AS rn FROM prashanth_subrahmanyam_catalog.dev_prashanth_subrahmanyam_evcr_bronze.tkt_coupon WHERE ORIG_AIRPORT_CD IS NOT NULL AND DEST_AIRPORT_CD IS NOT NULL AND FARE_BASIS_CD IS NOT NULL GROUP BY ORIG_AIRPORT_CD, DEST_AIRPORT_CD, FARE_BASIS_CD ) SELECT r.ORIG_AIRPORT_CD, r.DEST_AIRPORT_CD, r.coupon_count, f.FARE_BASIS_CD AS most_common_fare_basis FROM ( SELECT *, RANK() OVER (ORDER BY coupon_count DESC) AS rank FROM route_stats ) r LEFT JOIN fare_mode f ON r.ORIG_AIRPORT_CD = f.ORIG_AIRPORT_CD AND r.DEST_AIRPORT_CD = f.DEST_AIRPORT_CD AND f.rn = 1 WHERE r.rank <= 10 ORDER BY r.coupon_count DESC, r.ORIG_AIRPORT_CD, r.DEST_AIRPORT_CD
| Genie Status: MessageStatus.COMPLETED
| Genie Analysis: The top 10 origin-destination airport pairs by total number of coupons are shown, along with the most common fare basis code for each route. Notable data points include:
- **ANC to ATL**: 27 coupons, 
|
| Ground Truth SQL:
|   WITH route_counts AS (
  SELECT
    ORIG_AIRPORT_CD,
    DEST_AIRPORT_CD,
    COUNT(*) AS total_coupons
  FROM prashanth_subrahmanyam_catalog.dev_prashanth_subrahmanyam_evcr_bronze.tkt_coupon
  GROUP BY ORIG_AIRPORT_CD, DEST_AIRPORT_CD
  ORDER BY total_coupons DESC
  LIMIT 10
),
fare_basis_counts AS (
  SELECT
    ORIG_AIRPORT_CD,
    DEST_AIRPORT_CD,
    FARE_BASIS_CD,
    COUNT(*) AS fb_count,
    ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY ORIG_AIRPORT_CD, DEST_AIRPORT_CD ORDER BY COUNT(*) DESC) AS rn
  FROM prashanth_subrahmanyam_catalog.dev_prashanth_subrahmanyam_evcr_bronze.tkt_coupon
  GROUP BY ORIG_AIRPORT_CD, DEST_AIRPORT_CD, FARE_BASIS_CD
)
SELECT
  rc.ORIG_AIRPORT_CD,
  rc.DEST_AIRPORT_CD,
  rc.total_coupons,
  fbc.FARE_BASIS_CD AS most_common_fare_basis_cd
FROM route_counts rc
JOIN fare_basis_counts fbc
  ON rc.ORIG_AIRPORT_CD = fbc.ORIG_AIRPORT_CD
  AND rc.DEST_AIRPORT_CD = fbc.DEST_AIRPORT_CD
  AND fbc.rn = 1
ORDER BY rc.total_coupons DESC
|
